\DoxyCodeLine{00263\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00264\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ Drawing\ flag\ scheme:\ flags\ indicate\ drawing\ instructions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00265\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ for\ objects\ -\/-\/\ circles/lines/faces.\ Bits\ set\ as\ follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00266\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ 1\ \ -\/\ \ draw\ object?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00267\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ 2\ \ -\/\ \ fill?\ (4\ and\ 16\ imply\ 2,\ also)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00268\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ 4\ \ -\/\ \ off\ =\ foreground,\ on\ =\ background\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00269\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ (applies\ to\ interior,\ not\ border,\ overriden\ by\ bit\ 16)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00270\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ 8\ \ -\/\ \ border\ color?\ (default=foreground,\ else\ recorded\ color)}}
